# Controlled PCA

Each PC is found after controlling for prior PCs by selecting wines with
the smallest normalized distance in previous-PC score space, then
residualizing those earlier directions within that subset.

## PC1

- Subset size: `129971` | Max control distance: `0.0000`
- Explained variance in subset: `4.5187%`

It offers rich blackberry, black currant liqueur, anise and cedar flavors that are wrapped into firm tannins. The balance is really impressive. It's throwing some sediment already, so decant it.

Tasting note: From a three-acre block of the Valley View Vineyard just east of Solvang, this clonal selection shows cedar, black olive, black pepper and elderberry fruit on the tightly wound nose. Tart but ripe boysenberry fruit shows on the palate, spiced with peppercorn, more cedar and a slate-like minerality. Sticky tannins carry those flavors into the finish.

## PC3

### Positive examples

- `The Eyrie Vineyards 2012 Original Vines Pinot Gris (Dundee Hills)` (2.4847): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: The Eyrie Vineyards 2012 Original Vines Pinot Gris (Dundee Hills). Winery: The Eyrie Vineyards. Variety: Pinot Gris. Country: US. Province: Oregon. Region 1: Dundee Hills. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Original Vines. Critic score: 94. Listed price: 33.0. Tasting note: These “Original Vines” are in fact the oldest Pinot Gris vines in the country. They deliver exquisite details of earth and stone around a solid core of apple and Asian pear. It's bone dry, with exceptional depth.
- `Lange 2014 Reserve Pinot Gris (Willamette Valley)` (2.4157): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: Lange 2014 Reserve Pinot Gris (Willamette Valley). Winery: Lange. Variety: Pinot Gris. Country: US. Province: Oregon. Region 1: Willamette Valley. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Reserve. Critic score: 92. Listed price: 28.0. Tasting note: Production of this barrel-fermented reserve is roughly half of what it was in 2013, and in this instance, less is more. A sleek, sophisticated effort, it's bursting with flavors of pear flesh and skin, set against a wash of stony minerality. It's leesy, long and luscious.
- `Siduri 2006 Hawk's View Vineyard Pinot Noir (Willamette Valley)` (2.2740): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: Siduri 2006 Hawk's View Vineyard Pinot Noir (Willamette Valley). Winery: Siduri. Variety: Pinot Noir. Country: US. Province: Oregon. Region 1: Willamette Valley. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Hawk's View Vineyard. Critic score: 88. Listed price: 39.0. Tasting note: Kudos to Siduri for offering a serious Oregon Pinot Noir at alcohol levels (13%) reminiscent of Burgundy. It's a welcome tilt for the state that once was tagged as the new world's Burgundian hope, but which has sometimes seemed more like a California wannabe. Light and tart, this isn't a complex wine but brings the delicate nuances of the grape, with cranberry, citrus and strawberry.
- `The Eyrie Vineyards 2011 Original Vines Pinot Gris (Dundee Hills)` (2.2720): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Original Vines. Critic score: 92. Listed price: 22.0. Tasting note: Unique in style and sourced—these are the oldest Pinot Gris vines in the country—this young, yeasty, textural wine will surely continue to improve in the bottle. Give it a lot of breathing time, and complex layers of rock and fruit unfold. Jicama, cucumber, daikon radish...You get the idea. It tastes as clean and fresh as a mountain spring.
- `The Eyrie Vineyards 2014 Original Vines Pinot Gris (Dundee Hills)` (2.2303): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Original Vines. Critic score: 94. Listed price: 41.0. Tasting note: Planted in 1965, these are the oldest examples of this variety in the entire country. Splendid texture is a defining characteristic, with a yeasty, creamy mouthfeel. Ripe apples and toasted grains come through, as the wine extends through a long and powerful finish. Try it with grilled shrimp and a wine and butter sauce.
- `Erath 2006 Pinot Blanc (Willamette Valley)` (2.2247): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: Erath 2006 Pinot Blanc (Willamette Valley). Winery: Erath. Variety: Pinot Blanc. Winery: Duck Pond. Variety: Pinot Gris. Country: US. Province: Oregon. Region 1: Willamette Valley. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Sparkling. Critic score: 86. Listed price: 25.0. Tasting note: This is something you're not likely to see every day—a 10-year-old sparkling wine made from 100% Pinot Gris. Lacks the finesse and minerality of those Alsatian sparkling wines, but the flavors have been smoothed out over the years, and a pleasing toasty streak has crept into the tart pear skin fruit.
- `Ken Wright 2014 Bryce Vineyard Pinot Noir (Ribbon Ridge)` (2.2135): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: Ken Wright 2014 Bryce Vineyard Pinot Noir (Ribbon Ridge). Winery: Ken Wright. Variety: Pinot Noir. Country: US. Province: Oregon. Region 1: Ribbon Ridge. Region 2: Willamette Valley. Designation: Bryce Vineyard. Critic score: 96. Listed price: 63.0. Tasting note: This riveting wine displays the exceptional finesse and precision that fruit from this AVA can deliver. It's Pinot Noir expressed in the most subtle and demanding way. Beautifully orchestrated red fruits, sappy acids, lush spices, perfect balance and an immaculate mineral-soaked finish are all on display. Drink 2018 through 2030.

### Negative examples

Designation: Gran Reserva. Critic score: 84. Listed price: 17.0. Tasting note: Oaky stuff, with sawdust, roasted fruit and dark, floral berry aromas. The palate is surprisingly high in acidity and choppy, but lumbering oak adds some heft to the berry fruit and cola flavors that lead the charge. A bit smacking and medicinal, and herbal to boot.

### Positive examples

- `Bersano 2010 Badarina Riserva  (Barolo)` (1.0712): Wine review entry for preference modeling. Wine title: Bersano 2010 Badarina Riserva (Barolo). Winery: Bersano. Variety: Nebbiolo. Country: Italy. Province: Piedmont. Region 1: Barolo. Region 2: . Designation: Badarina Riserva. Critic score: 88. Listed price: 75.0. Tasting note: Aromas of French oak, roasted coffee bean, dark berry and menthol lead the nose. The ripe, full-bodied palate offers dried black cherry, licorice and a toasted note alongside assertive, close-grained tannins. You'll also notice the heat of evident alcohol that throws the finish off balance.
